				    <script>
                        require(["knockout", "jquery", "models/showcase-player", "underscore", "vanillaLazyLoad", "sidearm-responsive"], function (ko, $, ShowcasePlayer, _, LazyLoad) {
                            $(window).sidearmResponsive();

                            var vm = function () {
                                var self = this;

                                var defaultViewId = 1;
                                var overrideViewId = 2 || null;

                                self.views = ko.observableArray([
                                    { id: 1, text: "Roster View - List" },
                                    { id: 2, text: "Roster View - Grid" },
                                    { id: 3, text: "Roster View - Cards" },
                                ]);

                                var defaultView = 1;
                                var defaultRoster = $("#ddl_past_rosters").find("option:first-child").val();
                                var defaultSort = $('#ctl00_cplhMainContent_ddl_sort_options').find("option:first-child").val();

                                var selectedRoster = $("#ddl_past_rosters>option").map(function () { return $(this).val(); }).get().includes(location.pathname) ? location.pathname : null;

                                var viewIdParam = 2 || null;
                                var sortIdParam = "" || null;

                                var state = {
                                    view: viewIdParam || defaultView,
                                    roster:  selectedRoster || defaultRoster,
                                    sort: sortIdParam || defaultSort
                                };

                                self.activeView = ko.observable(state.view);
                                self.selectedView = ko.observable(state.view);
                                self.selectedRoster = ko.observable(state.roster);
                                self.selectedSort = ko.observable(state.sort);

                                self.updateActiveView = () => {

                                    // Probably a better way to handle this...
                                    // Remove pronunciation icon because the external script is going to add another one ever
                                    $('.earit_icon_image').remove();

                                    // If view is different, change it. Otherwise ignore.
                                    if (state.view == self.selectedView()) {
                                        return;
                                    }

                                    state.view = self.selectedView();
                                    self.activeView(state.view);

                                    window.history.pushState(state, "", buildQueryString() || location.href.split("?")[0]);
                                };

                                self.updateRoster = () => {
                                    if (state.roster == self.selectedRoster()) {
                                        return;
                                    }

                                    state.view = null;
                                    state.roster = self.selectedRoster();

                                    window.location = state.roster + buildQueryString();
                                };

                                self.updateSort = () => {
                                    // If sort is different, change it. Otherwise ignore.
                                    if (state.sort == self.selectedSort()) {
                                        return;
                                    }

                                    state.sort = self.selectedSort();

                                    window.location = location.href.split("?")[0] + buildQueryString();
                                }

                                self.activeView.subscribe(function(){
                                    setTimeout(function(){
                                        $.sidearm.sidearmResponsive();
                                        imglazyload.update();
                                        $(window).trigger('scroll');
                                    },0);
                                });

                                self.togglePlayer = function (data, event) {
                                    var $element = $(event.currentTarget),
                                        player_id = $element.data('player-id'),
                                        player_url = $element.data('player-url'),
                                        player_hide_bio = ((typeof $element.data('player-hide-bio')) !== 'undefined');

                                    if ($element.find('.sidearm-roster-player-extra').length == 0) {
                                        var _player = new Player(player_id, player_url, player_hide_bio);
                                        var $extra = $('#sidearm-roster-player-extra-original').clone().removeAttr('id');
                                        $element.append($extra);
                                        ko.applyBindings(_player, $extra[0]);
                                    }

                                    $element.toggleClass("show-extra").find('.sidearm-roster-player-extra').slideToggle(250);                 
                                };

                                var buildQueryString = () => {
                                    var queryString = "";
                                    var queryStringObj = {};

                                    if (state.view != null && state.view != defaultView) {
                                        queryStringObj["view"] = self.activeView();
                                    }

                                    if (state.sort != defaultSort) {
                                        queryStringObj["sort"] = self.selectedSort();
                                    }

                                    if (Object.keys(queryStringObj).length > 0) {
                                        queryString = "?" + new URLSearchParams(queryStringObj);
                                    }

                                    return queryString;
                                }

                                window.onpopstate = (event) => {
                                    var view = event.state.view;

                                    state.view = view;
                                    self.activeView(view);
                                    self.selectedView(view);
                                }

                                window.history.replaceState(state, "");
                            };

                            $(document).on("keydown", ".sidearm-roster-player-toggle", function(e) {

                                var $this = $(this),
                                    $parent = $this.parent(),
                                    key = e.which,
                                    shift = e.shiftKey;

                                if (key === 13 || key === 32) {

                                    setTimeout(function(){

                                        if ($parent.hasClass("show-extra")) {
                                            $parent.find('.sidearm-roster-player-extra a:visible, .sidearm-roster-player-extra button:visible').first().focus();
                                        }

                                    }, 350);

                                }

                            }).on("focusin", "a, button, select, input, option", function (e) {

                                var $this = $(this);

                                        e.preventDefault();

                                if ( $(".sidearm-roster-default-template .sidearm-roster-player.show-extra").length && $this.closest(".sidearm-roster-player-extra").length <= 0 ) {

                                    $(".sidearm-roster-default-template .sidearm-roster-player.show-extra .sidearm-roster-player-extra").hide();
                                    $(".sidearm-roster-default-template .sidearm-roster-player.show-extra").removeClass("show-extra");

                                }

                            });

				            var sharedVm = new vm();

                            var Player = function (id, url, hide_bio) {
			                    var self = this;

			                    self.isLoading = ko.observable(true);
                                self.id = id;
                                self.hideBio = hide_bio;
			                    self.stats = ko.observableArray();
			                    self.stories = ko.observableArray();
                                self.pressclips = ko.observableArray();
                                self.url = url;
			                    $.getJSON('/services/responsive-roster.ashx', { player_id: id, sport_id: '22', sport_shortname: 'wvball', year: '2022' }, function (response) {
			                        if (response === null || response.stats === null)
			                            self.stats(null);
			                        else {
			                            response.stats.map(function (stat) {
			                                self.stats.push(new Stat(stat));
			                            });
			                            self.stats()[0].selected(true);
			                        }

			                        if (response === null || response.stories === null || response.stories.length === 0)
			                            self.stories(null);
			                        else {
			                            var stories = ko.utils.arrayMap(response.stories, function (story) {
			                                self.stories.push(new Story(story));
			                            });
			                        }

			                        self.isLoading(false);
			                    });

			                    self.selectStatCategory = function (stat) {
			                        for (var i = 0; i < self.stats().length; i++)
			                            self.stats()[i].selected(false);
			                        stat.selected(true);
			                    };
			                };

			                var Stat = function (data) {
			                    var self = this;

			                    self.title = data.title;
			                    self.title_short = data.title_short;
			                    self.headings = data.headings;
			                    self.data = data.data;

			                    self.selected = ko.observable(false);                
			                }

			                var Story = function (data) {
			                    var self = this;

			                    self.id = data.id,
						        self.headline = data.headline,
						        self.teaser = data.teaser,
						        self.date = data.date,
						        self.image = data.image,
						        self.image_alt_text = data.image_alt_text,
						        self.url = data.url,
						        self.video = data.video
										        ? new ShowcasePlayer({ youtube: data.youtube, Archive: data.Archive })
										        : null;
			                }

                            var PressClips = function (data) {
			                    var self = this;

			                    self.id = data.id,
						        self.title = data.title,
						        self.author = data.author,
						        self.summary = data.summary,
                                self.date = data.date,
                                self.date = data.datedisplay,
						        self.image = data.image,
						        self.image_alt_text = data.image_alt_text,
						        self.url = data.url
			                }

			                ko.applyBindings(sharedVm, $('.sidearm-roster-templates-container')[0]);
			                ko.applyBindings(sharedVm, $('.sidearm-roster-header')[0]);

                            $(function() {

                                //download dropdown keyboard focus
                                $(document).on("focusin focusout", ".sidearm-roster-view .sidearm-roster-header-download ul a", function (e) {
                                    if (e.type === "focusin") {
                                        $(this).closest(".sidearm-roster-header-download").addClass("sidearm-hover");
                                    } else if (e.type === "focusout") {
                                        $(this).closest(".sidearm-roster-header-download").removeClass("sidearm-hover");
                                    }
                                });

                            });

                            var imglazyload = new LazyLoad({
                                elements_selector: ".lazy",
                                data_src: "original"
                            });

                        });
                    </script>

<script>
    require(['jquery'], function($) {
        var scrollTimer = null;
    
        function hide_ads() {
            $('html').addClass('sticky-leaderboard-is-hidden');
        };
        
        function scrolled() {
            scrollTimer = null;
            if($(window).scrollTop() > 300){
                $('html').addClass('sticky-leaderboard-is-hidden');
            } else {
                $('html').removeClass('sticky-leaderboard-is-hidden');
            }
        };
    
        setTimeout(
            function(){
                $(window).scroll(function(){
                    if (scrollTimer) {
                        clearTimeout(scrollTimer);
                    }
                    scrollTimer = setTimeout(scrolled, 500);
                })
        }, 5000);
    });
</script>

<!-- /ko --></script>
                    <script>
                        window.preloaded_templates_are_rendering = true;

                        require(['knockout'], function (ko) {
                            function register_custom_loader(component, vm_name, template_name) {
                                if (document.getElementById('template-' + (template_name || component) )) {
                                    var custom_loader = {
                                        getConfig: function(name, callback) {
                                            if (name === component + '-component') {
                                                componentConfig = {
                                                    template: { element: 'template-' + (template_name || component) },
                                                    viewModel: { require: 'components/' + (vm_name || component) }
                                                };
                                                callback(componentConfig);
                                            }
                                            else {
                                                callback(null)
                                            }
                                        }
                                    };

                                    ko.components.loaders.unshift(custom_loader);
                                }
                            }

                            register_custom_loader('ads', 'promotions', 'promotions');
                            register_custom_loader('dfp', 'evergreen', 'evergreen');

                            register_custom_loader('navigation');
register_custom_loader('events');
register_custom_loader('results');
register_custom_loader('search');

                            
                            window.preloaded_templates_are_rendering = false;
                        });
                    </script>

<script>
    var host_element = document.querySelector(".buu2x3env-modal__text-host");
    host_element.href = window.location.href; 
    host_element.innerText = window.location.hostname; 

    function close_banner() {
        var CookieDate = new Date;
        CookieDate.setTime(CookieDate.getTime() + 1 * 3600 * 1000 * 24);
        document.cookie = "sidearm-adblock-banner_consent=true; expires=\"" + CookieDate.toGMTString() + "\";";
        document.querySelector(".buu2x3env").remove();
    }

    var consent_button = document.querySelector(".buu2x3env-banner__consent");

    consent_button.addEventListener("click", function() { close_banner(); });

    require(['config'], function(config) {
        require(['jquery', 'knockout', 'cookie', 'text'], function ($, ko, cookie, text) {
            $(function () {   
                //disable check for Siteimprove scans
                if (navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase().indexOf('siteimprove') < 0) {
                    
                    if (cookie.get_cookie('sidearm-adblock-banner_consent')) {
                        return;
                    }

                    var deferred = $.Deferred();
                    $.ajax({
                        type: "HEAD",
                        async: true,
                        url: "/components/js/analytics.js",
                    }).done(function(message,text,jqXHR){
                        deferred.resolve();
                    })
                    .fail(function(err){
                        show_ad_blocker_blocked_modal();
                        deferred.reject();
                    });

                    deferred.then(function(success) {
                        $.get('/common/templates/dfp/dfp-component-template.html')
                            .then(function (response) {
                            }, function (error) {
                                show_ad_blocker_blocked_modal();
                            });
                    }, function (error) {
                        show_ad_blocker_blocked_modal()
                    })
                    .fail(function(){
                        show_ad_blocker_blocked_modal()
                    });

                    function show_ad_blocker_blocked_modal() {
                        var modal = document.querySelector('.buu2x3env');
                        modal.style.display = 'flex';
                        modal.querySelector('.buu2x3env-banner__consent').focus();
                    }
                }
            });
        });
    });
</script>
